export default class Counter  {
  @State
  count = 0

  increment(delta: number = 1) {
    this.count += delta
  }

  decrement(delta: number = 1) {
    this.count -= delta
  }
}

    @ $mol_action
    static patch_snap() {
      const patch = { ...this.patch }
      this.patch = {}
      return { ids: Object.keys(patch), patch }

    @ $mol_mem
    @ $mol_action
    static kc() {
      const oidc = this.oidc()
      const clientId = this.client_id()

      const params: KCCOnfig = {
        url: oidc.url,
        realm: oidc.realm,
        clientId,
        token: this.token_access(),
        idToken: this.token_idt(),
        refreshToken: this.token_refresh(),
        redirectUri: this.redirect_url(),
        enableLogging: true,
        timeSkew: 0,
        minValidity: this.minValidity()
      }

      const kc = $mol_wire_sync(this).kc_async(params)

      this.token_access(kc.token)
      this.token_refresh(kc.refreshToken)
      this.token_idt(kc.idToken)

      return kc
    }
